All endpoints use the same paths across versions.\n\n### 2. **ConnectorStateInfo and TaskStatus Response Handling**\n\n**File**: `/workspace/kafka--0753c489/connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java`\n\nKey classes:\n- **ConnectorStateInfo** - The API versioning strategy relies on backward-compatible schema evolution rather than separate endpoint versions.\\n\\n### REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\n**Main Connector Resource Handler** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/ConnectorsResource.java):\\n- Primary handler for all connector-related REST operations\\n- Registered at @Path(\\\"/connectors\\\") with single implementation serving all API consumers\\n- Handles connector CRUD operations, status queries, task management, and restart operations\\n- Methods: listConnectors, createConnector, getConnector, getConnectorConfig, getConnectorStatus, getConnectorActiveTopics, resetConnectorActiveTopics, putConnectorConfig, patchConnectorConfig, restartConnector, stopConnector, pauseConnector, resumeConnector, getTaskConfigs, getTaskStatus, restartTask, destroyConnector, getOffsets, alterConnectorOffsets, resetConnectorOffsets\\n\\n**Internal Cluster Resource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/InternalConnectResource.java and InternalClusterResource.java):\\n- Separate handler for inter-worker communication at @Path(\\\"/connectors\\\")\\n- Handles internal-only operations: putTaskConfigs (POST /{connector}/tasks) and fenceZombies (PUT /{connector}/fence)\\n- Used for cluster-internal communication, not exposed to external clients\\n\\n### API Version Strategy: Schema Evolution Instead of Path Versioning\\n\\n**No Separate v1/v2 Endpoints**: The codebase does not implement separate /v1/connectors or /v2/connectors paths. Instead, versioning is handled through:\\n\\n1. **Response Schema Backward Compatibility**:\\n   - ConnectorStateInfo.AbstractState includes: state (string), worker_id (string), trace (string, non-empty only on errors), version (string from plugin)\\n   - TaskState.TaskState extends AbstractState and adds: id (int)\\n   - Error responses use consistent ErrorMessage format: {error_code: int, message: string}\\n   - Optional fields are marked with @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_EMPTY) or custom filters, allowing old clients to ignore new fields\\n\\n2. **Storage Layer Versioning** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/KafkaConfigBackingStore.java):\\n   - TARGET_STATE_V0: Original schema with single \\\"state\\\" field (for backward compatibility with connectors written before STOPPED state existed)\\n   - TARGET_STATE_V1: Enhanced schema adding optional \\\"state.v2\\\" field (contains actual state: STOPPED)\\n   - Dual-field approach: Both \\\"state\\\" (PAUSED for stopped connectors) and \\\"state.v2\\\" (actual STOPPED) are written to satisfy old and new workers\\n   - During deserialization: reads \\\"state.v2\\\" if available, falls back to \\\"state\\\" for older records\\n   - This strategy allows mixed-version clusters where old workers don't support STOPPED state\\n\\n### Status Response Schemas\\n\\n**Task Status Response** (returned by getTaskStatus endpoint):\\n- ConnectorStateInfo containing:\\n  - name: String\\n  - connector: ConnectorState (state, worker_id, trace, version)\\n  - tasks: List<TaskState> where each TaskState has (id, state, worker_id, trace, version)\\n  - type: ConnectorType enum\\n- State enum values: UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED\\n- STOPPED state added later for connectors only (never for tasks)\\n\\n**Connector Status Response** (returned by getConnectorStatus endpoint):\\n- Same ConnectorStateInfo structure but typically used for connector-level status\\n- Includes all tasks associated with the connector\\n\\n**Error Response Schema**:\\n- Consistent across all endpoints: {\\\"error_code\\\": int, \\\"message\\\": String}\\n- Mapped by ConnectExceptionMapper from exceptions: ConnectRestException, NotFoundException, AlreadyExistsException, WebApplicationException\\n- HTTP status code + error_code both present in response\\n\\n### Version Routing Logic\\n\\nNo explicit version routing exists in the codebase. Instead:\\n\\n1. **Single Registration** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java):\\n   - ConnectRestServer extends RestServer and registers resources once\\n   - regularResources(): returns Arrays.asList(RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource)\\n   - adminResources(): returns Collections.singletonList(LoggingResource)\\n   - No variant resources for different API versions\\n\\n2. **REST Server Setup** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/RestServer.java):\\n   - Uses Jersey (jakarta.ws.rs) and Jetty (embedded HTTP server)\\n   - JacksonJsonProvider for JSON serialization/deserialization\\n   - ConnectExceptionMapper handles all exception-to-response conversions\\n   - No Accept-Version, X-API-Version, or similar headers are processed for routing\\n\\n3. **Configuration** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/RestServerConfig.java):\\n   - No API version configuration properties\\n   - Listeners configured via HTTP/HTTPS URIs without version specifiers\\n\\n### Key Findings\\n\\n**Versioning Approach**: Kafka Connect uses **transparent backward compatibility** rather than explicit API versioning:\\n- All clients use same endpoints regardless of Connect/client version\\n- New optional fields in responses are safely ignored by older clients\\n- Storage layer maintains dual representations for incompatible state transitions (e.g., STOPPED state addition)\\n- Plugin versions are included in responses (version field in task/connector states) but are informational only\\n\\n**No v1/v2 Split**: Despite the task's reference to v1 and v2 handlers, the actual implementation maintains a single unified API that evolves through optional field addition and storage-layer compatibility strategies. This is a common pattern for HTTP APIs serving diverse clients with varying versions.\\n\\n**Response Type Information**: Version information in responses comes from plugin implementations (ConnectorState.version, TaskState.version) and Kafka Connect version (ServerInfo.version), not from API versioning.\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":778,"cache_read_input_tokens":68691,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":778},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"58d1ca87-7efd-4a45-9f46-470e21c1f5c4","uuid":"32b0003f-3076-4b98-8a07-fad87b3e23fc"}
